<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Explore California Like a Local</h2>



<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b3fbc0d36b6b6be3bd737a5b30f9bf86" style="color:#51575c;font-size:18px"><em>I have lived, traveled, and breathed California&nbsp;<strong>for over 20 years.</strong> I was still living at home with my parents when we took a family vacation out west. The minute this native East Coaster stepped foot in California, I knew I was home. In my 20s, I moved to&nbsp;San Francisco&nbsp;and now reside in&nbsp;Los Angeles, but I&#8217;ve seen nearly every inch of California in my 20 years here. Let me help you explore California&#8217;s diverse natural beauty and cultural and recreational opportunities.</em></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns8_38bb8b-64"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn8_4d7a3c-dd kt-btn-size-small kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://californiagirltravels.com/about/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">READ MORE</span></a></div>
</div>

<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h4 class="wp-block-heading">Hello, I&#8217;m Jessica.</h4>



<p style="font-size:18px">I&#8217;m a California-based travel blogger. I&#8217;ve called this sunny state home for over 20 years and can&#8217;t get enough of its beauty. When I&#8217;m not jetting off, I&#8217;m at home with my partner and our two lazy cats (I&#8217;m a dog person, long story).</p>



<p style="font-size:18px">But no matter how far I roam, California is where my heart is. From <strong>Catalina Island</strong> to <strong>San Francisco</strong> and <strong>Napa Valley</strong> to <strong>Los Angeles</strong> and <strong>Santa Barbara</strong>, the diversity, the ocean breeze, and the laid-back vibe keep me grounded.</p>



<p style="font-size:18px">Writing is my second love after travel/chocolate. Beyond travel, I&#8217;m all about supporting entrepreneurs in their pursuit of a dream life.</p>
